 Bihar Chief Minister Nitish Kumar said on Saturday that the post of governor should be abolished in all states as it is not necessary to continue in the current federal democratic system
 pradhanmantri narendra modi kii adhyakshata main yahaan yojit antarraji parishad kii baithak main unki tippanee tab aayi he jab haal main ucchtam nyaayalay ne arunachal pradesh ke rajyapal kii rajya main congress sarkaar kii barkhaastagi ko lekar kadi aalochana kii thi tathaa kuch vipakshi partiyon ke shashan vaale rajyon ne rajbhawanon par centre ke ishaare par raajnneetik rup se kaary karne kaa aarope lagaaya he
 JDU president Kumar said that if it is not possible to abolish the constitutional post, then its discretionary rights should be curtailed
 unhone yah bhi kaha ki kisi bhi rajya ke mukhyamantri kii rajyapal kii niyukti or use hataane main bhoomika honi chahie
 He said, "in the current federal democratic system, it is not necessary to continue as Governor
" yadi use samaapt karnaa sambhav nahin to hamaare vichaar se rajyapal kii niyukti se jude praavdhaanon kii spasht rup se vyakhya honi chahie or use paardarshee banaaya janaa chahie
 "apart from this, the Chief Minister of the state should also be consulted and the criteria set by the Sarkaria Commission should be followed in the appointment of the Governor," he said

 lashkar aatanki naved jet pichley dinon srinagar ke aspataal se faraar ho gaya tha
 Although the police have not confirmed it yet, cctv's photographs of the three suspects are being identified
 philhal pahchaan ke liye sthaneey logon kii madad lee ja rahi he
 Although Lashkar has condemned the assassination of Shujaat Bukhari, security agencies believe that it may be part of the terror organization's strategy
 police ne maamle kii jaanch shuru kar di or hamalaavaron kii pahchaan kii ja rahi he
 Mobile numbers have also been issued by the Jammu and Kashmir Police to give information related to the attackers
 iske saath hi ab police is sisitivi footage kii jaanch kar hamalaavaron tak pahunchane kii koshish main juty he
 In two photographs released by the police, three people are seen going on bikes with their faces covered
 pehle bhi bukhari par ho chuke hai jaanaleva hamaleshujaat bukharipar isse pehle bhi kai baar jaanaleva hamale ho chuke hai
 In July 1996, the terrorists held him hostage in Anantnag for seven hours
 saal 2000 main jaan se maarane kii dhamkee ke baad bukhari ko police suraksha di gai thi
 In 2006 too, Bukhari was attacked with murder
 ek saal pehle hi pakistani aatankiyon se unhen dhamkee mili thi
 He was then given X-class security, with two security personnel stationed with him
 shujaat bukhari bharat-paak shanti vaarta or kashmir vivaad ko sulajhane ke liye lagaataar sarkaar ke saath kadam se kadam milakar chal rahe the
 Along with this, his newspaper Rising Kashmir is called the voice of the valley
 jaan ke khatre ke baavjood wo hameshaa kaha karte the ki bandook kaa dar dikhaakar unki kalam ko shant nahin karaayaa ja saktaa
 a two-day strike of public sector bank employees across the country began on Wednesday to protest against the government's policy of privatization
 mangalvaar ko mukhya shram ayukta es ke mukhopadhyaay or united forum of bank union (yuafbiyu) ke netaaon ke bich baatcheet vifal ho jane ke baad bankkarmiyon kaa hadtaal par janaa tay ho gaya tha
 Around 60,000 bank employees in Tamil Nadu are involved in the strike
 yahaan ke yuafbiyu ke sanyojak si ech venkatachalam ne bataaya ki kuch nijee bainkon ke saath sarkari bainkon kii shakhaaen hadtaal kii vajah se band rahengi or ham aaj chennai main ek juluus bhi nikaalenge
 Banks are also closed in Kerala and employees are performing in front of banks across the state
 vyavsaayiyon kaa kahana he ki do din tak bainkon ke band rahane se unhen kaaphi kathinaayee kaa saamana karnaa padegaa
 It is to be noted that various unions of banks have been opposing the Foreign Direct Investment (FDI) in the banking sector

 In the conclusion of the Jamiat Ulema Hind National Working Committee meeting to review the Supreme Court's decision on the Ayodhya case, Chairman Maulana Arshad Madani has said that the decision of the court is beyond comprehension
 kanoon or nyaay kii najar main vahaan babari masjid thi or he or qayaamat tak masjid hi rahegi phir chaahe usko koi bhi naam yaa swaroop kyon na de diya jaae
 Madani said that one thing is clear from the court's decision that the mosque was not built by breaking a temple nor did it take place at a temple site
 court kii is baat se musalamaanon ke daaman par laga ye daag dhul gaya jisamen mandir todakar yaa mandir kii jagah par masjid banane ke aarope lagate rahe
 Discussing the reconsideration petition, Madani said that Jamiat has formed a panel which will conclude from the lawyers and academics on the basis of facts and evidence whether to file a reconsideration petition
 madani ne court ke faisle ko lekar kaha ki ek tarah to court ne ye mana ki masjid ke andar murti rakhana or phir use todna galat tha phir bhi court ne jameen unheen logon ko de di jinhone masjid main murti rakhi phir masjid ko tod diya
 On the issue of 5 acres of land by the court, Madani said that Muslims have never been fascinated by the land and this land has been given by the court to the Sunni Waqf Board and my advice is that the board should not accept the land
 ek sawaal ke jawaab main madani ne kaha ki babari masjid mudde ko international court main le jane kii baat bemaani he, court hamaara he, mulk hamaara he or ham supreme court ke faisle kaa sammaan karte hai
 We will take action according to the constitution and law of the country
 ant me madani ne kaha ki agar masjid ko naa todaa gaya hota to kya court ye kahati ki masjid todakar mandir banaaya jaae? hamen is baat kaa santosh hai ki court ne mana ki masjid ko mandir todakar nahin banaaya gaya lekin afsos he ki sabooton or tathyon ke vipareet court ne puri jameen ram lalaa ko de di
 Madani said that when the court called the mosque demolition illegal and considered it a violation of law, then the criminals involved in this crime should be heard daily
 kendriya vitt mantri arun jetali ne shuukravaar ko kaha ki sabhi rajyon ke vitt mantri vastu evam seva kar (jiesti) jald lagu karne ke paksh main hai
 After a pre-budget meeting with the state finance ministers, Jaitley said that all states are in favor of speedy implementation of GST
 sarkaar kii yojana ek april 2016 se jiesti lagu karne kii he
 Last week, the government introduced the GST Bill in the Lok Sabha
 sarkaar ke mutabik 1947 ke baad se yah akelaa sabase mahatvapurn kar sudhaar he
 Jaitley has already told Parliament for uninterrupted implementation of this bill that within three years, the central government will pay the outstanding compensation amount of Rs 34,000 crore to the states
 shuukravaar ko hui baithak main jetali ne yah bhi kaha ki kuch rajya chaahate hai ki rajkoshiya uttardaayitv evam bajet prabandhan adhinium 2003 (etharabime) kii seemaa badhaai jaae taaki rajya or adhik karj le saken
 The FRBMA Act was passed by the Parliament
 iskaa uddeshy vittiya anushaasan ko sansthagat karnaa, rajkoshiya ghate ko kam karnaa or vyapak aarthik prabandhan main sudhaar laana tha
